This Appendix Addendum contains\ndrawing revisions, tables of run conditions, model photographs,\ntables of pressure measurements,\nand plots\nof charging station profiles and model pressure distributions.\nNew Instrumentation\nInstrumentation\nwas added to the model for measuring static pressure distributions on the core\ncowl outer flow surface downstream of the fan throat. The purpose was to measure the pressure\ndistributions and interactions between the base, chevron, and tab nozzle trailing edge devices. Three axial\nrows of 10 pressure taps each were added at circumferential\nangles of 300, 330, and 345 degrees. Model\nstations for these pressure taps are documented on the following pages and on the detail drawings.\nThis instrumentation was not present in the original model design. Therefore the tubing was\nrouted out of the core hardware and onto the inner fan duct air flow surface in a low Mach number region.\nIt was covered with metallic tape. The tubing crossed the fan duct flow at 315 degrees. A sheet metal\nshield was used to form a strut for the 30 instrumentation tubes in an inline fashion. A total temperature\nrake/plug was modified by removing the temperature rake and slotting the plug to route the\ninstrumentation out of the model. The sheet metal strut and tubes were all soldered to this plug. Existing\nPSI system ESP modules mounted in the sting were reconfigured to measure the new instrumentation.\nOne new T24 core nozzle was fabricated with static pressure instrumentation\n(2212-404). Tests\nwere first done with the core tabs in place. Then half the tabs were cut off to locally simulate a baseline\ncore nozzle. The tabs were cut off by hand with a Dremel tool parting disk.\nTest Matrix and Conditions\nThe table below presents the test matrix. The chevron fan nozzle was first tested at the normal\nposition with part top at top dead center(3T24Co).\nThis positioned the fan chevron sharp point tip in line\nwith a core tab protruding into the fan flow at the top dead center position. Next the fan chevron nozzle\nwas rotated 22.5 degrees to position the fan chevron valley directly in line with the core tab at top dead\ncenter(3T24C22.s).\nTarget test conditions were cruise point "A" (Pt7/Pa=2.6, Pt7/PtS=l.083,\nMath # =0.8).\n\nTest\nSequence\n1\n2\n3\n\n7\n\nNA SA/CR--2001-2\n\nDescription\n3 (core)(_an)\n3T24B\n3T24Co\n3T24C 2_,5\n3B\'Cz2.5\n3B\'Co "\n3B\'B\n\n10712\n\nData\nPoint\n201.02\n201.03\n202.02\n203.01\n204.01\n205.01\n206.01\n\nCore\n\nPt7/Pa\n\nFan\n\nDrawing #\n2212-404RevB\n2212-404RevB\n2212-404RevB\n2212-404RevB\n2212-404RevC\n2212-404RevC\n2212-404RevC\n\n167\n\nDrawing\n2078-001\n2078-001\n2078-003\n2078-003\n2078-003\n2078-003\n2078-001\n\n(@\n(@\n(@\n(@\n\n--.2\n\nPtT/Pt8\n\nMach\n\n2.598\n2.601\n2.607\n\n1.094\n1.064\n1.087\n1.082\n1.085\n1.091\n1.O80\n\n.796\n.794\n.800\n.787\n.789\n.803\n.801\n\n#\n\n0 deg.)\n22.5 de_. )\n22.5 deg.)\n0 deg.)\n\nz58t\n2.591\n2.626\n2.621\n\n2212taps.xJs, ch6& 1O_TAPS\n\n10/29/98\n\nJob 2212: NASA AST NOZZLE TESTS\nInstrumentation\nChannel\n\nLocations\n\n]\n\n6&10 C, )re Charqlqq _taption\nPressure Tap no.
